Eden's Lobbying in Europe: Visits to Paris and Rome; Italy Hints Abyssinian Issue Should Not Be Raised; Naval Issue Mainly for International Conference 36

(Paris) British Minister Without Portfolio Anthony Eden arrived here at 3:05 PM tonight. It is expected that tomorrow he will discuss the European military and political situation with the French side, and explain the reasons for the UK's establishment of a naval agreement with Germany. (National Telegraph, 20th)

(London) Minister Without Portfolio Anthony Eden's trip to Europe will also include a visit to Rome. According to official circles, Eden will discuss naval armament issues with French Prime Minister Laval, as well as the next steps to be taken regarding the conclusion of a Western European air pact. He will then go to Rome to discuss the same matters with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini. The British government made this announcement after Mussolini sent a letter agreeing to Eden's proposal to visit Rome. (Reuters, 21st)

(London) According to public announcements here, after visiting France, Eden will also proceed to Rome to meet with Mussolini to explain Britain's policy toward Germany. Although official reports only mention naval and air force issues, reliable sources suggest that Eden will also present new solutions to Italy regarding the Abyssinian issue. (National Telegraph, 20th)

(Rome) Semi-official sources indicate that when British Minister Without Portfolio Anthony Eden comes to Rome to hold talks with the Italian government, the Abyssinian issue will absolutely not be mentioned. As for the naval issue, Italy opposes all arms races and advocates convening an international conference to determine the tonnage limits of major naval powers. Otherwise, if countries regain the freedom to rearm, naval tonnage will inevitably continue to increase without end. (Havas, 21st)

Anglo-French Talks Begin

(Paris) Anglo-French talks began at 11:30 AM this morning. In addition to British Minister Without Portfolio Anthony Eden and French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval, those representing Britain included British Ambassador to France Sir George Clerk and British Embassy Counselor Campbell. Those representing France included Secretary-General of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Léger and Director of Political Affairs Massigli. It is reported that this morning's talks were entirely limited to the Anglo-German naval agreement. After the talks, Laval hosted a luncheon. The talks will resume at 3:00 PM in the afternoon. (Havas, 21st)

(Paris) After this morning's cabinet meeting, Sir Anthony Eden immediately met with Laval. This is given much importance here. Eden arrived in Paris at 7:00 PM last night and resided at the British Embassy. Newspapers this morning stated that this meeting is extremely important for international peace and the future of Franco-British relations. Wireless reports expressed optimism, saying that what is already clear is that the bond between Britain and France, after this open and honest negotiation, will become even stronger. This meeting is not limited to discussing the Anglo-German naval agreement, but will also involve the entire range of European armaments and security issues. (National Telegraph, 20th)

(Paris) Regarding the Anglo-German naval agreement, newspapers believe that unless Britain can propose a plan for closer cooperation with France on security issues to eliminate the impact of this separate agreement, Eden's trip may not be enough to appease French sentiment to a considerable degree. Moreover, since the naval issue has been separated from the overall security plan to form an agreement, newspapers are not keen on discussing a Western European air pact before the issues listed in the February 3rd London Declaration are resolved. The Petit Parisien reported: "The principles on which French foreign policy is based should not change. The various issues included in the February 3rd London Declaration cannot be partially resolved in a perfunctory manner. Therefore, if Eden only raises the issue of the air pact without mentioning others, the strong opposition of France and Italy is inevitable." The Echo de Paris reported: "Since the Anglo-German naval agreement was established on the 18th of this month, creating a new situation, we have had to make other plans, such as refusing to discuss the Western European air pact until the overall issue is resolved." (Havas, 21st)

Main Objectives of Eden's Visit to Italy 37

(London) The government has proposed to Italy that Minister Without Portfolio Anthony Eden, after finishing his business in France, should go to Rome to hold talks with the Italian government, considering (1) the Abyssinian issue, (2) the naval issue, and (3) the Western European mutual assistance air pact. This proposal has been accepted by Italian Prime Minister Mussolini. It is generally understood that the British government, due to misunderstandings between Britain and Italy regarding the Abyssinian issue, first wants to eliminate them. After Eden arrives in Italy, he can take the opportunity to explain matters frankly to Mussolini to ensure a peaceful resolution to the Italo-Abyssinian dispute. British political figures are now planning to grant Italy significant economic interests in Abyssinia and build a railway between Italian Somaliland and Eritrea, passing through Abyssinian territory, to satisfy Italy's demands and avoid the outbreak of war. As for the naval issue, Eden will explain the content of the Anglo-German naval agreement to Mussolini. Since experts from both Britain and Germany have agreed on a seven-year period for the realization of the German naval plan, Italy and France may not immediately resume their freedom to build warships. Finally, Eden will explain the progress of negotiations on the Sky Locarno Pact and the Eastern European Pact, and jointly consider with Mussolini the Danube Pact, which is generally considered the most difficult to establish. (Havas, 20th)

Britain Actively Augmenting Air Force Strength, Adding 150 Aircraft, Increasing Fighter Speed 38

(London) The British Air Force, having been approved by Parliament last month to expand the Aviation Department, is actively proceeding. According to the Daily Telegraph, the Aviation Department has already ordered several batches of aircraft, including two batches totaling 150 aircraft. The remaining batches are still under price negotiation. The aircraft to be built include several types of bombers, coastal reconnaissance aircraft, and training aircraft. Daytime bombers must have a range of 1,000 miles, while nighttime bombers must have a range of 2,000 miles. However, the speed of fighter planes will increase to between 275 and 300 miles per hour. It is expected that the capabilities of general aircraft will be developed, and civilian transport aircraft that can be transferred for military use will also have the same development. (Reuters, 21st)

British First Lord of the Admiralty Explains Reasons for Anglo-German Agreement to the House of Commons; Acknowledges German Naval Reconstruction as a *fait accompli*; Fixed Ratio May Avoid Competition; Believes This Move Benefits the Conclusion of a General Agreement 39

(London) First Lord of the Admiralty Monsell today stated in the House of Commons the reasons why Britain had to conclude a naval agreement with Germany, stating that Britain, at the beginning of the talks, accepted Hitler's proposal that the ratio of British to German fleets should be fixed at 100 to 35. The British government believes that this is not only beneficial to future relations between the two countries but also facilitates the conclusion of a general agreement on the future limitation of naval armaments. The British government also considers this move to be very important, as it can permanently eliminate the possibility of Anglo-German naval competition. Once this competition begins, it will inevitably hinder the interests of British autonomous territories. The agreement is also indeed beneficial to the naval affairs of other countries. Some may say that the two countries should not have concluded this agreement, but we must face the facts. (Cheers from the audience) We must face the important practical problems. The fleet that Germany is currently building has exceeded the limits of the Treaty of Versailles. What we are doing now is to agree with Germany on a scope for the impact that Germany's unilateral decisions may have. We firmly believe that this move will ultimately benefit all naval countries in the world. If we had hesitated to accept Germany's proposal, we would have made a big mistake. Fortunately, we did not do so, and we are very gratified. Some say that Britain should not handle the naval limitation issue alone, setting aside the land and air disarmament issues. The British government can never endorse this view. Naval limitation treaties have existed for many years. If we cannot renew treaties to replace the existing ones, the harm will be great. This move does not imply that the British government will no longer actively strive to conclude land and air armament treaties if a general naval limitation treaty is concluded in the future. In fact, the British government considers preventing international competition in all three types of armaments to be a matter of utmost importance. Monsell also responded to questions, saying that the government will continue to talk to other naval powers, but he does not know when the countries that signed the naval treaty will be able to hold a plenary meeting. Prime Minister Baldwin also responded to questions about when the House of Commons should choose a day to debate the agreement, saying that Leader of the Opposition Lansbury should prepare for discussion when the First Lord of the Admiralty's official salary is presented for consideration. (Reuters, 21st)

German Special Envoy Meets with British Prime Minister; Franco-Soviet Pact is the Topic of Discussion 40

(London) According to news reported by the Daily Telegraph, the purpose of Prime Minister Baldwin's meeting with German naval representative Ribbentrop yesterday was to discuss Germany's return to Geneva. This statement has recently been denied by official circles. It is reported that the talks between the British and German representatives, in addition to the naval issue, were only about the Franco-Soviet Mutual Assistance Pact. Britain and France had previously sent notes to the German government, explaining Germany's objections to the Franco-Soviet Mutual Assistance Pact. It is reported that Britain has urged Ribbentrop to ensure that Germany responds to the Anglo-French notes as soon as possible. As for the outcome of Baldwin's talks with Ribbentrop, it will be notified to French Prime Minister Laval by Minister Without Portfolio Anthony Eden, who is currently in Paris. (Havas, 21st)

(London) The Daily Telegraph reported that Prime Minister Baldwin mentioned the issue of Germany's return to the League of Nations during his meeting with Ribbentrop, the chief representative of the German naval delegation. Germany is now preparing to return to the League of Nations under the following two conditions: (1) concluding a Western European Air Pact; (2) the impact of mutual assistance pacts on the Locarno Pact should be satisfactorily explained by the signatory countries of the Locarno Pact. (Havas, 21st)

(London) Rumors have circulated that during talks between German representative Ribbentrop and British cabinet members, the possibility of entrusting a Portuguese colony to German rule was considered. This information has recently been explicitly denied by officials. However, according to sources in Berlin, this approach may be sufficient to compensate for Germany's abandoned plan to expand eastward. (Havas, 20th)

Experts Continue Discussions on Details; Agree to Limit National Battleships to 25,000 Tons; German Naval Plan to Be Implemented Within Seven Years 41

(London) Ribbentrop, the chief representative of the German naval delegation, went to 10 Downing Street this morning to meet with Prime Minister Baldwin for about an hour. This was the first meeting since the German delegation arrived here. The two delegations then also met to continue negotiating the details of the naval agreement. The next meeting is scheduled for Friday and Saturday, so the German delegation will be unable to leave London until Sunday at the earliest. (National Telegraph, 20th)

(London) After the Anglo-German naval agreement was established, naval experts from both countries met yesterday to discuss the tonnage of different types of ships. According to information obtained by the Daily Telegraph, the German representative completely agreed with the British proposal that the maximum limit for battleships of all countries in the future should be 25,000 tons. Both sides have also agreed on limiting cruiser tonnage to around 7,000 tons. (Havas, 21st)

(London) Regarding the Anglo-German naval talks, it is now reported that naval experts from both countries have agreed that the German naval plan will be implemented within seven years. British representatives are now trying to get Germany to agree not to build the full tonnage during this period, leaving a small amount to be completed after 1942. It is generally hoped that Germany will announce its shipbuilding plan until 1942 soon, so that British naval experts can use it as a basis when holding talks with naval representatives from France, Italy, and Russia. (Havas, 20th)

German Newspapers Detail Shipbuilding Program 42

(Berlin) According to estimates published in local newspapers, if Germany builds warships to the maximum limit permitted by the Anglo-German agreement, Germany's fleet will consist of the following: (1) Battleships: six new 25,000-ton ships and four existing 10,000-ton ships; (2) Battlecruisers: five new 10,000-ton ships to the maximum limit, but there are currently no such ships; (3) Light Cruisers: a total of 67,000 tons, in addition to six existing 6,000-ton old ships, five new 6,000-ton ships or eight new 4,000-ton ships can still be built; (4) Destroyers: There are currently twelve 800-ton destroyers, and another 43,000 tons can be built, but the agreement stipulates that this tonnage can be transferred to building light cruisers instead of destroyers, as there is no clear distinction between these two types of ships at present; (5) Aircraft Carriers: Can be built to a limit of 51,000 tons. Germany currently has no such ships, so two 22,000-ton aircraft carriers can be built; (6) Submarines: approximately 23,000 tons, but Germany promises not to exceed 45% of the total tonnage of British submarines. The size of submarines varies greatly, so it is impossible to predict the exact number of submarines Germany will build at this time. Germany is currently building twelve 250-ton submarines, but the London Agreement stipulates that each submarine can reach 2,800 tons. (National Telegraph, 20th)

Tokyo Authorities Study Countermeasures 43

(Tokyo) The full text of the naval agreement concluded as a result of the Anglo-German talks arrived at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on the 20th. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs immediately held a joint meeting with the Ministry of the Navy at 4:00 PM to discuss future countermeasures. The meeting adjourned at 7:00 PM. (Dentsu Telegraph, 21st)

Abyssinian King Asks League of Nations to Pay Attention to Italian Acts of Aggression; Italian Troops Continuously Arrive in East Africa, Endangering Abyssinia's Independence and Integrity; Suggests Sending Personnel to Investigate the Truth 44

Capital of Abyssinia: Abyssinian King Selassie sent a note to the Council of the League of Nations, stating that Italy is constantly increasing its troops and transporting military supplies to East Africa, while repeatedly making outrageous remarks that endanger Abyssinia's independence and integrity, in an attempt to prove the correctness of its acts of aggression. This makes the East African war unavoidable. Therefore, Abyssinia requests the League of Nations to pay attention. (National Telegraph, 21st)

(Geneva) The Abyssinian government has once again sent a note to the Secretary-General of the League of Nations, protesting against Italy's attitude and suggesting that a neutral observer committee be immediately appointed to go to the border areas between Abyssinia and Italian territories to inspect the actual situation and investigate the truth of the incident, so as to submit a report to the Council of the League of Nations. The Abyssinian government promises to provide all necessary assistance to these observers to enable them to perform their duties, and all expenses will be borne by Abyssinia. Abyssinia's love of peace can be seen from this. (Havas, 20th)

(Rome) According to news from Geneva yesterday, the government of Abyssinia has once again sent a note to the Secretary-General of the League of Nations, protesting against Italy's attitude and suggesting that a neutral inspection committee be immediately appointed to go to Abyssinia, especially the Socotri land bordering Italy, to investigate the truth of the incident, so as to submit a report to the Council of the League of Nations. Semi-official sources here consider this move to be erroneous and believe that the League of Nations will not accept it. Otherwise, Italy will undoubtedly develop antipathy towards the League of Nations. (Havas, 21st)

Italy Protests to Abyssinia for Insulting National Flag 45

Rome: It was announced here today that Italy has formally protested to Abyssinia, saying that an Abyssinian aviator recently insulted the Italian national flag. (National Telegraph, 20th)

Black Sea: Red Navy Exercises 46

Sevastopol: A team from the Black Sea Fleet is currently conducting naval combat exercises in the Black Sea with various warships, submarines, air force, and land fortifications. The exercises are commanded by Commander of the Black Sea Fleet Gyeranov. All Red Navy soldiers and officers have demonstrated their excellent training. The Black Sea Fleet calmly and skillfully responds to attacks from batteries, torpedoes, the air, and underwater. In the evening, sound films, concerts, and various recreational activities are held to entertain the officers and soldiers on board. (TASS, 20th)

Leningrad: A huge naval sailing ship is undertaking a 3,890-kilometer sea voyage from Leningrad to Astrakhan. The event is organized by students from the Naval Academy and the Military and Political Academy, and the entire journey is expected to be completed on the 29th. (TASS, 20th)

French Government Issues Decree Extending Military Service Term 47

(Paris) During today's session of the Chamber of Deputies, Prime Minister Laval read out the government's decree extending the term of military service, stating that during this period of troop shortage, new recruits who enlisted in April 1935 will continue to serve for six months after their one-year term of service expires. Soldiers of all levels who enlisted from October 1935 to the end of 1939 will have their military service extended by one year. If security organizations and arms limitation negotiations are unsuccessful, there is no hope of reducing the term of military service. The government has also decided that half of the soldiers whose service expires in April this year will continue to serve until half of the new recruits who enlisted in April have received the minimum amount of training. The decree also expressed gratitude to French volunteers for being discharged from military service by July 1. (National Telegraph, 20th)

(Paris) Extreme left-wing members of the Chamber of Deputies criticized this decree. Prime Minister Laval replied, "If you members of the Chamber of Deputies were to take office, you would probably take even bolder measures, because as long as the collective security system is not complete, we must take all measures to defend peace." (Havas, 20th)

Austerity in Government Expenses to Be Implemented in October 48

(Paris) The Chamber of Deputies today resolved that the expenses of all administrative departments will be reduced by 20% from the beginning of October. In addition, the funding that the state provides to the social insurance system will be reduced from 82 million francs to 22 million francs. This austerity measure will not harm the beneficiaries, because large sums have been converted into funds in the past five years. (Reuters, 21st)

A Beautiful Young Woman Suddenly Appears in the Chamber of Deputies; Climbs Down from the Balcony on a Rope; Asks for Attention to the Danger of French Population Decline; Police Drag Her Out, Causing Disorder 49

(Paris) While members of the Chamber of Deputies were speaking eloquently and passionately debating national affairs today, a beautiful young woman suddenly emerged from the balcony, using a long rope to climb down, quietly entered the members' seating area and sat down. The entire Chamber was surprised to see a sudden visitor and fell silent. Then, shouts of condemnation arose. Attendants rushed into the area and dragged the woman out. The order of the meeting was greatly disrupted, and the meeting was suspended. When the police questioned the woman, she replied that she wanted to draw the attention of national legislators to the serious danger of French population decline. (Reuters, 20th)

Spain: Replenishing National Defense Plan; National Arms Are Under Government Control 50

Madrid: Minister of the Army Robles declared to Congress last night that all national armories should be directly under the jurisdiction of the Ministry of the Army to replenish national defense. Any armory with more than 300 employees and less than 1,500 employees will set up a mobilization bureau, managed by an active-duty officer. As for the four-year plan to replenish Spain's national defense, which the cabinet discussed yesterday, the president has signed a secret order stipulating that the production rate of munitions should be increased to meet military needs. From now on, the raw materials for munitions used by the Spanish National Defense Force will be manufactured by national industries. (National Telegraph, 20th)

(London) Prime Minister Baldwin recently declared in the Privy Council that the position of Undersecretary for Foreign Affairs will soon be established, and it is possible that Lord Cranborne, Minister Without Portfolio Eden's Parliamentary Secretary, will be appointed to this new position. (London) Overseas Dominions Minister Thomas made a declaration in the House of Commons, stating that the overseas dominions fully agree with British foreign policy as a whole and believe that if Britain does not implement the announced measures to defend the security of the empire, it will be neglecting its duty and disregarding its obligations to the empire. (Havas, 20th)

German Veterans Group Arrives in Britain and is Welcomed; Old Battlefield Combatants Shake Hands Today 52

(London) A tour group organized by German veterans arrived at the Port of Dover today and was warmly welcomed by representatives of the British Ex-Servicemen's Association. This is the first time such a group has arrived in Britain since the European War. According to its leader, who spoke to reporters, although Germans opposed Britain during the European War, they are now very happy to enter Britain and shake the hands of friends. The visit of this veterans group to Britain is a response to Prince Edward's call to eliminate the old evils of war. The people of both countries warmly agree with Prince Edward's words. (Reuters, 20th)

(London) Representatives of German veterans, invited by the British Ex-Servicemen's Association, have now arrived in Britain. After landing at the Port of Dover today, they went to Brighton to attend a welcome meeting organized by the local branch of the Ex-Servicemen's Association. (Havas, 20th)

Yugoslav Political Upheaval: Cabinet Submits General Resignation; Little Entente Conference Postponed 53

Belgrade: Yugoslav Prime Minister Jevtić suddenly resigned today. Subsequently, the ministers of the army, finance, public works, and commerce also successively withdrew from the cabinet. The reason for this resignation is mainly due to internal political infighting. (National Telegraph, 21st)

Belgrade: After the resignation of the Yugoslav Jevtić government last night, Dr. Maček, a prominent leader of the Croat people, was invited today to participate in consultations on the formation of a new cabinet. Maček has accepted this invitation. Maček's efforts to seek Croat autonomy have lasted for many years and have long been feared by the government. In 1933, he was accused of conspiracy to split the Kingdom of Yugoslavia and sentenced to three years in prison. He was released after the assassination of King Alexander. The government's resignation was caused by the withdrawal of three Serbian and Croat cabinet members from the government. After the regent prince and the speakers of both houses of parliament held late-night consultations, they issued an invitation to Maček. Jevtić's trip to Europe has now been canceled, and the conference of the Three Little Entente countries has also been postponed. (Reuters, 21st)

Belgrade: The cabinet of Prime Minister Jevtić of Yugoslavia suddenly submitted its resignation on the eve of the political conference of the Little Entente countries. Although this was unexpected, after the recent re-election of the Yugoslav parliament, the parliamentarians of various opposition parties led by Farmers' Party leader Dr. Maček refused to attend, at which time it was generally predicted that this would cause a cabinet crisis. Subsequently, the government parliamentary group in parliament, led by the ministers of internal affairs and justice, openly debated with the opposition parties, while those who advocated loyal cooperation between various constructive elements within the country did not generally agree, and even the Croatian party within the government did not agree with breaking with the opposition parties. Therefore, for several days, various factions have been holding negotiations in a difficult atmosphere in parliament, and the leaders of the Slovenian People's Party, Bishop Krek, and the leader of the Bosnian Muslims, Spaho, suddenly came to the capital, which led to the political crisis. The Jevtić cabinet then submitted its resignation so that the regent could examine the parliamentary situation to make appropriate decisions. After the cabinet resigned, the political conference of the Little Entente countries was postponed indefinitely. It is also heard that after the cabinet resigned, opposition leader Maček has come to the capital and may be received by the regent. (Havas, 21st)

(London) The British government has formally notified governments with relations to the Far East about the dispatch of the chief economic advisor, Sir Otto Niemeyer, to China. It also hopes that each country will send experts to China to gather in one place and discuss the overall situation. (Reuter, 21st)

(Tokyo) At 4:35 this morning, central Japan experienced a severe earthquake that impacted a wide area, but caused no damage. The epicenter was located near a certain mountain about 60 kilometers north of Tokyo. (Reuter, 21st)

International Labor Conference Passes 40-Hour Work Week Convention Draft 57

(Geneva) The International Labor Conference recently passed a draft general convention on reducing working hours with a majority of 81 votes against 33. It also passed a resolution with a majority of 75 votes against 27, requesting governments to take appropriate measures to allow employers and employee groups to directly negotiate changes in wage treatment as much as possible. It also requested governments to periodically submit reports to the International Labor Bureau on the various measures taken to implement the 40-hour work week and maintain workers' living standards. (Havas, 20th)

France Halts Cash Outflow: Bank Discount Rate Reduced 58

(Paris) The discount rate of the Bank of France has recently been reduced from 6% to 5%. According to the bank's official announcement, the outflow of cash has completely stopped, the bank's gold reserves have increased by 28 million francs, and the amount of banknotes in circulation has decreased by 75,018,282 francs. Therefore, the discount rate has been reduced. (Havas, 20th)

Swiss Finance Minister Meyer recently officially stated that the Swiss central bank currently has gold reserves of 1,162,000,000 Swiss francs and has issued banknotes totaling 1,247,000,000 Swiss francs, with a cash reserve ratio of 93%. At the beginning of March this year, the cash reserve ratio was 135%. Due to the trend of cash outflow, the discount rate will remain at 2.5%. (Havas, 20th)

Japan's Next Year's Budget: Military Expenditure Reaches 1.2 Billion Yuan; Air Force Expansion Fee 100 Million Yuan; Army 600 Million, Navy 500 Million 59

(Tokyo) In addition to the Army Ministry's next fiscal year budget of over 490 million yuan, it plans to request 100 million yuan for air force expansion fees and material preparation fees, bringing the total army expenditure to 600 million yuan. The Navy Ministry, in addition to over 530 million yuan, has a total of 600 million yuan for warship construction fees and land and sea preparation fees. In particular, the Navy Ministry needs to expand its naval plans due to the abolition or revision of the Washington and London Treaties. Therefore, the next fiscal year's national defense expenditure for the army and navy will inevitably reach over 1.2 billion yuan. The difficulty for the government in compiling the budget lies in reconciling national defense expenditure with finance. It is noteworthy how Finance Minister Takahashi will handle this issue between the opinions of the parliament and the cabinet deliberation committee.

On the afternoon of the 20th, Army Minister Hayashi held a meeting with Vice Minister Hashimoto and Military Affairs Bureau Director Nagata to discuss the policy direction for the Army Ministry's next fiscal year budget request. As a result, Army Minister Hayashi will explain the army's opinions at the cabinet meeting on the 25th. The content is roughly as follows: The Army Ministry considers the current state of national finances and strives to implement budget savings. However, given the current international situation and the need to maintain domestic military industry capabilities, 200 million yuan is required for combat material preparation fees and national defense expansion fees, and 86 million yuan for emergency air force expansion fees. As for the Manchurian Incident expenses and security work, which have not yet been completed, and the construction of permanent facilities for the Kwantung Army, a necessary budget of 150 million yuan is required, the same as this year. The Army Minister will change the explanation of the content of other new plans to seek approval. Therefore, the Army's expenditure for the next fiscal year will reach approximately 600 million yuan. (Jiji, 20th)

Roosevelt's Wealth Redistribution Plan: Declaration of War Against Opponents of the New Deal; Annual Tax Revenue Could Increase by 1 Billion 60

(Washington) Congress today saw President Roosevelt's new tax proposal and was completely unclear whether there was a request for immediate action. The Senate Finance Committee refused to approve some amendments to the 500 million yuan increase in temporary taxes, which caused a setback to the government's plan. It is expected that President Roosevelt will soon clarify this confusing situation. Treasury Secretary Morgenthau stated today that he would not estimate how much revenue the new taxes could bring in unless Congress asked this question. According to private estimates, the revenue from the new taxes is approximately between 750 million yuan and 1 billion yuan per year. Important critics on Wall Street are mostly cautious and unwilling to say much about President Roosevelt's plan to tax wealth redistribution. Some say that the government wants to use the extra taxes, gift taxes, and inheritance taxes to reduce the national debt. This is clearly a mixed method of being radical and steady. However, some people also point out that this is just another step in exploiting the rich. Generally, people expressed concerns about the proposal to increase corporate taxes according to the progressive method, because the taxes on some industries, such as public utilities and railways, are already extremely heavy. If they are burdened further, it will restrict the development of corporate businesses. Some people also say that the new tax plan is simply a declaration of war against business leaders and wealthy people who oppose the New Deal. The authorities stole the politically startling claims of the radicals led by Senator Long and others to prepare for future election competition. This move can be said to be nimble. President Roosevelt's new proposal has now met with opposition, and even those who support the government do not fully agree with it. During the term of this Congress, the President's proposal may not be passed. According to rumors from those close to President Roosevelt, the President may issue another unexpected message today. It is heard that President Roosevelt is currently considering a new national recovery plan to advance simultaneously with the tax plan. Its purpose is to increase the purchasing power of the people. However, an essential condition for this plan is that there must be a definite and unwavering interpretation of interstate commerce that can be tested as to whether it is in conflict with the Constitution. (Reuter, 20th)

International Commercial Telegram - Special Commercial Telegram from Reuters on June 21st - 61

Gold and Silver

Today's gold price in London is 141 shillings, 2.5 pence, up 1 penny.

The London silver market fell today. The spot price is 32 pence 125, and the futures price is 32 pence 375, both down 1875. American, Chinese, and speculators all bought in, with no sellers. Mount Lyell bar futures loosened today due to the low London silver price. The September opening price was down 26 pounds.

Exchange Rates

The London foreign exchange market was stable this morning. The opening exchange rate between the United States and Britain was 4 yuan, 9 jiao, 3 fen, 375, the same as the closing price between the United States and Britain yesterday. It fell 1875 within the first hour, and recovered 125 at noon. The market situation was quite stable. It continued to rise 3125 at 2 p.m., to 4 yuan, 9 jiao, 3 fen, 75, 375 higher than the opening price.

The opening price between Britain and France was 74 francs 59, down 3 pounds. It continued to fall 8 pounds within one hour, and recovered 6 pounds at noon. It rose again 6 pounds at 2 p.m., to 74 francs 63, 4 pounds higher than the opening price.

Cotton and Wheat

New York cotton opened slightly higher this morning. The July price was 12.59, up two points, because it was heard that Agriculture Secretary Wallace has agreed that new cotton in 1935 can be used to offset debt. However, the amount of debt and how much can be offset per pound have not been announced, as it needs to wait until the cotton production is determined before it can be announced. The agricultural product adjustment law passed by the House of Representatives stipulates that Agriculture Secretary Wallace will determine the export subsidy fee, but this decision is not mandatory and can be changed by the Senate. The cotton market changed slightly later, and the price was not much different from the opening.

The July price for Liverpool cotton at 1 p.m. today was 6.34, up 6 points.

The Liverpool wheat market was relatively stable this morning. The July price at 1 p.m. was 5 shillings, 3 pence, 875, up 1 penny.

The Mangalore wheat market was sluggish and unchanged this morning. Grains were slightly lower than yesterday's closing, but the weather was unstable, and the wheat market started a new buying trend, resulting in a firm market price. Grains rose one point due to reports of cloudy weather and reduced inventory.

Rubber

The London rubber market was stable today. The transaction price for July and September at noon was 6 pence 125, up 0.0625.

The New York rubber market was very stable. The opening price rose three points, and the price remained firm afterwards. It is heard that sellers are limited, and sentiment is bullish.

Securities

The trend of the New York securities market yesterday changed this morning. Most securities rose, exceeding yesterday's closing price. Merchants were less pessimistic about the legislative future, because President Roosevelt's tax proposal caused a reaction in Congress yesterday. The opening price of securities was still maintained later, and the general trend was upward, with cheerful sentiment. The average price of the Dow Jones 30 industrial securities was 117.68, up 44 points.

Antioch: Chalice Discovered; Object from the First Century Roman Era 62

(London) The Palestine Biblical Archeological Society received a report today from the archeological team engaged in excavating antiquities in Antioch, stating that the team had discovered a small box containing a glass cup, which appeared to be a product of the first century Roman era. According to experts, the cup is likely to be the chalice used by Christ and his disciples at the Last Supper. If so, the object that has been sought for centuries has now been obtained. Shandong Economic Crisis: Local Products Stagnant, Prices Plummet; All Banks and Firms Unanimously Tighten Credit 89

Jinan Correspondence: In recent years, rural bankruptcy and industrial and commercial collapse in our country, and the people's livelihood is becoming increasingly difficult, creating extreme social unrest. Shandong, which is controlled by foreign economic forces, is no exception. Furthermore, local products are stagnant, finance is stagnant, and all industries are on the verge of bankruptcy. The recent situation of finance and local products in Jinan is described below:

Banks and Firms Only Take In, Do Not Lend Out

There are dozens of banks and firms in Jinan, including the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, the Central Bank, the Minsheng Bank, the China Industrial Bank, the Continental Bank, the Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank, the Donglai Bank, the Zhonglu Shandong Commercial Bank, and the Zhejiang Industrial Bank, as well as the Ping City Official Money Bureau and silver shops. Their main business is mortgage lending on local products. The major local products in Shandong are cotton, peanuts, and grains. This year, due to the stagnant sales of local products and the plummeting prices, the mortgaged goods in most local product firms cannot offset the original mortgage amount. Therefore, all banks and firms have adopted a tightening policy, only taking in and not lending out. It is heard that the Bank of China, which has the most mortgage lending, has also received orders from its head office that the amount of lending must not exceed five million yuan.

Cotton Stagnant, Cotton Yarn Weak

Cotton is the largest local product in Shandong. When the new cotton was launched this year, it was still active. American cotton was 55-56 yuan per dan. Recently, sales have been sluggish, and prices have fallen again and again. The price per dan is only around 40 yuan. More than 130,000 bales of cotton are stored in the market, piling up and not moving, which has a great impact on the market. Not only are the flower shops and cotton merchants crying bitterly, but the financial sector is also increasingly affected. The price of each yarn has fallen from more than 190 yuan to more than 180 yuan. Today, the 18th, news came from the Qingdao Exchange that the price of cotton yarn has plummeted by 10 yuan per piece due to the impact of Japanese yarn dumping. The price has fallen to more than 170 yuan, which is also an unprecedented tragedy.

Peanuts Stagnant, 200,000 Bales in Storage

Peanut kernels are also a major local product in Shandong. The initial opening price this year was 7.7 yuan per dan. Currently, the price has fallen again and again, with each dan only worth 5.4 yuan. There are 200,000 bales of peanut kernels in storage in the Jinan market. Although some merchants from Tengxian and Yanzhou have recently purchased a portion, preparing to sell them in the fall, it is also extremely empty, because sales are fundamentally stagnant and it is difficult to be optimistic.

Wheat Prices Fall and Rise Again

As for the province's grain, it is still relatively peaceful. A few days ago, wheat was 4.7 yuan per dan, then fell to around 4 yuan. In the past day or two, it has risen again to 4.12 yuan. As of today, the 18th, there are a total of 4,550 tons of wheat in storage in the market. (18th)

Site of Spring and Autumn Qi State Capital: Shang Dynasty Bronzes Discovered, Along with Several Pieces of Jade 90

Jinan Correspondence: Taigong was enfeoffed in Qi during the Spring and Autumn period, and established his capital in Linzi. Linzi has a long history and is of important value in archeology. The Central Research Institute and the Provincial Library jointly formed the Shandong Ancient Site Research Association. They first excavated the ancient Tan State near Jinan, and then excavated the former site of Tengxian Tengxue. It was originally planned to continue excavating the Qi capital in Linzi, but it was delayed due to various reasons. It is heard that recently, the ancient city north of Linzi City, which is said to be the former site of the Qi capital, had several kinds of antiques dug out of the ground after the rain the other day by villagers tilling the fields. There were a total of seven pieces of bronze ware, including tripods and plates. Their volume is larger than those commonly seen. There is a lot of soil on them. It has not yet been discovered whether there are any characters. Antique dealers, hearing the news, flocked to investigate. The villagers regarded them as rare goods, asking for 8,000 yuan. Buyers have already paid 800 yuan, but the deal has not yet been completed. It is also heard that there are several pieces of jade, including an ancient jue as large as a plate.

Guangdong Province, East River: Bandit General of Nanshan Eliminated - Numerous Guns and Captured Bandits Seized - 91

Shantou Correspondence: The bandit nest of Nanshan in the East River of Guangdong Province is located at the junction of Chaoyang, Puning, and Huilai counties. The mountains are steep, and there are 120 villages of various sizes, covering 120 square li. The highest organ of the Communist bandits of the East River was located in this mountain. After the purge in the 16th year of the Republic of China (1927), the bandit leader Peng Pai led the Communist bandits from Haifeng and Lufeng to twice capture Huilai City. After the bandits were severely suppressed by government troops, they fled into the mountains. Tens of thousands of people in the mountain villages were subjected to "reddening." The garrison Zhang Division once blockaded Nanshan for more than a year, and sent teams into the mountains to patrol, killing more than 3,000 bandits successively. The bandit disaster began to be quelled. Zhang Division then established reclamation offices, recruited refugees, implemented the Baojia system, opened roads, and dispatched two special task force brigades to be stationed in the mountains for a long time to protect traffic and public security. This spring, Zhang Division moved to southern Jiangxi. Before the Deng Division took over, the remnants of Zhang Dingcheng's troops from western Fujian, under pressure from the Central Army, sneaked into Chaozhou Prefecture from the mountains between Fujian and Guangdong, colluded with the remnants of Nanshan bandits, and resumed their activities, looting everywhere. The people suffered greatly. When the Deng Division moved to Chaozhou and Shantou from Anyuan and Xunwu, it reorganized its troops to suppress the bandits in the mountains. On the one hand, it convened a pacification meeting of Chenghai, Chao'an, and Jieyang counties to step up the work of bandit suppression and Baojia in various counties. The military officers who entered the mountains to search for the remaining bandits have repeatedly won victories, seizing a total of 169 long and short guns, two light machine guns, and capturing 152 bandits, including pseudo-Soviet special committee members. 214 pseudo-special committee members, secretaries, section chiefs, directors, and bandits were killed. Sixteen organs such as the bandit military affairs office, repair factory, political capital prison, etc. were destroyed. Eighty-five innocent men and women who had been seized were rescued. Twenty-eight bandits surrendered and thirty-eight long and short guns were brought in by surrendering bandits. Three district and township chiefs who supplied the Communist bandits were executed by firing squad, and one village head who hid bandits was detained for investigation. Currently, the troops are going deep into the mountains to search various caves and are expected to completely eliminate the bandits soon. The bandit area of Fenghuang Mountain on the border of Rao Ping is also being blockaded and encircled by Zeng Youren's Brigade. It is reported that the remaining bandits in the mountains have sneaked back into the mountains of Pinghe and Zhao'an on the Fujian border. (16th)

Total Silkworm Cocoon Production in Jiangsu Province 96

Since the Jiangsu Provincial Sericulture Improvement and Management Committee was organized by the Department of Construction to improve the sericulture industry in Jiangsu Province, significant results have been achieved. Because the quality of silkworm eggs is good, the quality of fresh cocoons produced is higher than that of cocoons produced in other places, and the drying and reeling loss is also shorter. This year's spring market collected more than 350,000 yuan in improvement fees, and a total of 87,000 dan (market weight) of dried cocoons were produced. Based on the calculation of drying one dan of cocoons from 300 jin of fresh cocoons, this is equivalent to 134,000 dan of fresh cocoons. However, farmers in Wujiang, Wuxian, Yixing, Liyang, and other places mostly bake fresh cocoons and reel silk themselves. Wujiang County has the most, with 10,000 zu of fresh cocoons, Wuxian 10,000 dan, and Yixing and Liyang a total of about 5,000 dan, Wuxi 1,000 dan, totaling about 270,000 dan. Currently, the market price of dried cocoons is 90 yuan per dan (Sima weight). A plan should be implemented as soon as possible.

Changzhou: Villager Murdered, Autopsy Conducted 97

Li Ren, the son of Guo Yiyuan, a resident of Fuzhen Town in the third district of Wujin County, went out to cut grass with a young shop assistant from a neighboring household on the morning of the 18th but did not return home. Prosecutor Guan Junjie led the autopsy officials to the village on the morning of the 20th to conduct an autopsy at the scene. The autopsy revealed that the body had two ropes tied around it, but there were no marks. There were multiple stone injuries on the back, indicating that he had been suffocated to death before being thrown into the harbor with stones. The father of the deceased pleaded for justice. Prosecutor Guan, considering the seriousness of the murder case, agreed to arrest the murderer and investigate the case, and instructed the family to prepare a coffin for the burial.

Unified Management of Summer Cocoon Purchases 102

The Department of Construction, in order to manage and purchase summer cocoons that will soon be on the market, has formulated measures that have been approved by the provincial government meeting. The regulations stipulate: (1) Cocoon merchants who purchase summer cocoons should apply to the local county government for approval before opening for business; (2) An improvement fee of 6 jiao per dan of fresh cocoons should be paid; (3) After cocoon merchants collect dry cocoons and pay the improvement fee, the county will issue a certificate for transportation. If there are arrears, the cocoons may be detained; (4) Other management matters are the same as the spring cocoon measures. All counties have been ordered to announce this so that everyone is aware, so as to avoid competitive bidding, monopolies, or suppressing cocoon prices, in order to maintain the silk market.

Conference of Directors of Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Bureau: Proposals Reviewed Yesterday, to be Discussed at General Meeting This Morning, Minister of Finance Kong Arrived Yesterday to Deliver Speech 103

The conference of directors of stamp, tobacco and alcohol tax bureaus from various provinces under the Tax Administration held a subcommittee meeting yesterday to review the proposals. It was decided to convene a general meeting this morning to present them for discussion. Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi made a special trip to the meeting yesterday afternoon to give a speech. Details are as follows:

Two Groups Review

The Review Committee was divided into two groups. The first group consisted of Zhao Xi'en, Sheng Shengyi, Jing Youyan, Jing Xuxin, Huang Zupei, Xue Futian, Yang Duo, Dong Zhongding, Hong Yi, Jiang Yongyi, Fang Yunxian, Li Jialin, Guo Yushan, and Xu Zhijun. Zhao Xi'en was designated as the chairman to review proposals (A), (B), and (C). The second group consisted of Ding Chungao, Wang Guanghui, Tang Yan, Qu Dacheng, Fu Zhengshun, Zhou Jiechun, Tang Shi, Chen Jun, Lu Zongqian, Xu Huiyu, Cheng Luyu, and Xu Yangzheng. Ding Chungao was designated as the chairman to review proposals (D), (E), and (F).

Minister of Finance Arrives

The two groups held meetings simultaneously starting at 9 am yesterday. The first group met in the reception room of the National Tariff Commission of the Customs Administration, and the second group met in the reception room of the Tax Administration. At 11:40 am, Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi arrived and was received by Wu Qiding, the director of the Tax Administration. The two subcommittees were notified to suspend their review, and they gathered at the reception room of the Tax Administration, where Minister Kong delivered a speech. They adjourned at about 1 pm. The two groups continued their meetings at 2:30 pm and adjourned after completing their review at about 5 pm. The general meeting will be convened starting at 9 am this morning to discuss the proposals.

Summoning and Instruction

Minister Kong delivered a speech, saying: "The purpose of convening this tobacco and alcohol tax conference of directors of stamp, tobacco, and alcohol bureaus from various provinces has been explained by Director Wu at the opening. My visit today is not to give a lecture, but to listen to the reports of the directors on the tax revenue situation and what contributions they have to make to future improvement measures. At this time of national crisis, all of you are intellectuals and naturally have a strong sense of patriotism. Moreover, you are responsible for the national revenue, so you must do your best to rectify it and enrich the national treasury. Finance is the lifeblood of the country, and it all depends on taxes, which come from the people, but should not harm the people. At present, the main sources of income are customs duties, salt taxes, and consolidated taxes. Judging from the results, the consolidated tax is easier to manage, the tax source is concentrated, and since its implementation, it has made progress year by year, and the revenue has increased day by day. However, the stamp, tobacco, and alcohol taxes have deep-rooted malpractices and are not easy to eliminate. Although they are under the jurisdiction of the Tax Administration, there is still no effective result. Since the stamp tax was entrusted to the post office for sale last year, the revenue has been better, while the tobacco and alcohol taxes remain the same. The reasons for this are nothing more than that those who are in charge are perfunctory and the supervisors are not persistent. In short, the director of the bureau bears the heavy responsibility of the country and cannot just be clean and self-disciplined. They should earnestly rectify matters and pay attention to whether their subordinates are engaging in corruption. If there are any disobedient people, they should be punished. I have always been sincere to my subordinates and will not replace them without a reason. I hope that all directors will be energetic and do their best to rectify and eliminate malpractices with resolute measures in order to enrich the country and benefit the people. If we want to talk about industry, economy, and national defense construction, none of them can be done without money. At this time of national difficulty, all directors should be able to understand this and do their best to alleviate the national crisis. Those who can be loyal and responsible will have unlimited prospects. Those who are perfunctory, irresponsible, or corrupt will not be excused even if they are acquaintances of this minister. I hope everyone will pay attention."

Loans will be started from today, with ordinary households receiving 5 to 10 yuan, and special households receiving no more than 30 yuan. Farmers in the county who are in genuine need of fundamental loans and have difficulty raising funds can apply for loans from the branch offices in their respective districts.

Yangtze River Public Pooling by Six Companies: Employing Chinese and Foreign Experts, Forming Freight Committee, Yichang Line Also Included 111

The scope of the Yangtze River public pooling alliance of six companies is expanding, and there are no restrictions on companies joining. The ships of Nissin Kisen Kaisha, which have suspended sailing, may also join the apportionment. Foreign companies such as Butterfield & Swire and Jardine Matheson's ships above Hankou, such as the Yichang and Changsha lines, are also included in the public pooling alliance. Not only are they accommodated as much as possible, but it is also agreed that the iron barges of the six companies on the Yangtze River in the middle and lower reaches shall also be allowed to join the pooling scope. This has been specified in the nineteen-article contract that has been officially decided.

Business Overview: The implementation of public pooling on the Yangtze River was initiated by the Ministry of Communications, and the state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company strongly promoted it. According to the survey and statistics of the six companies, the tonnage of each ship must be determined by the ship surveyor and listed as the recognized tonnage. The more ships there are, the greater the volume of goods transported, and the more cost-effective the business will be. After it is implemented on July 1, the most beneficial company among the six companies is Butterfield & Swire, followed by Jardine Matheson, followed by Sannorth, and Nissin. China Merchants Steam Navigation Company ships are not as beneficial as Sannorth because they have more passenger seats and less cargo volume. The amount of cargo for public pooling is based on the exchange of cargo manifests between the six companies, and the customs general manifest is the basis.

Determining Experts: Although the calculation of public pooling on the Yangtze River by the six companies is based on 50% of the total tonnage of the ships, the ships are of different sizes and the amount of cargo varies, making the calculation of apportionment extremely difficult. It is difficult for non-experts to calculate accurately. Therefore, after discussion by the six companies, two Chinese and Western accounting specialists were specially hired to be responsible for calculating the public pool accounts. The Western expert has been appointed Thompson, and the Chinese expert has been appointed Xi Yushu. Both are paid a salary of 1,000 yuan. The letters of appointment have been issued.

Freight Meeting: The six companies have also agreed to form two groups of meetings composed of important officials selected from within each company. Group A is composed of managers and directors of each company to discuss all major issues concerning business and the alliance. Group B is composed of business directors and chief clerks selected by each company. A freight committee is formed within Group B to discuss the increase in round-trip shipping costs and the determination of various cargo commissions after public pooling. It is currently being actively organized.

Interruption of Sino-Japanese Submarine Cable Line: Wireless Telegraph Reaches Smoothly, International Radio Station Intends to Reorganize Sino-Japanese Circuits, Reducing Telegraph Rates to 65 Cents per Word 112

According to the Xinxin News Agency, there are two types of telecommunications between Shanghai and Japan: wireless and submarine cable. Since the 18th of this month, the submarine cable between Nagasaki and Shanghai of the Japanese Telegraph Bureau has been interrupted. Telegrams between China and Japan are received and sent by the International Radio Station on Renji Road, and are sent and received as soon as they arrive. General users are satisfied. It is reported that since the opening of the Sino-Japanese wireless circuit of the station last summer, it has been intending to reorganize. All the machines are of the latest automatic type. In addition to Chinese and English telegrams, it also receives Japanese telegrams. The staff has been specially trained. It is also heard that since this month, the telegraph rates have been reduced. The cost of sending ordinary telegrams to Japan is only 65 cents per word. Furthermore, for Chinese telegrams sent to various parts of Japan, the text, whether clear or secret, can include seven numbers in each group of characters, which is counted as one word. The name of the receiving station and the name and address of the recipient are written in Chinese, regardless of the number of words, all counted as one word. As for Japanese telegrams, every seven Japanese letters are counted as one word. The name of the receiving station and the name and address of the recipient are written in Japanese, regardless of the number of words, also counted as one word. The International Radio Station has special newspaper for this type of telegram for the convenience of all sectors.

Aivelo Company Hosted Reporters Yesterday: Test Ride of the Autogiro Aircraft, Equipment All Improved, Very Fast Takeoff and Landing, Suitable for Passengers, Cargo, Bombing, and Reconnaissance 113

The latest British-made Autogiro aircraft was brought to Shanghai from Hong Kong a few weeks ago by Mr. Bennett, manager of the Far East Aviation Company at No. 88 Museum Road in this city. It was immediately assembled temporarily in the hangar of the China Aviation Corporation in Longhua. After a test flight the day before yesterday afternoon, yesterday afternoon at about 3 p.m., Chinese and foreign reporters were invited for a public demonstration, personally piloted by Mr. Bennett. The aircraft is a land-based type, about 10 feet long, with a single engine (140 horsepower). The fuselage is painted yellow, with black stripes at the tail end. It has no front wings, and the rear wings extend to 45 feet. At the top of the aircraft, there is an upward-pointing rotor with three blades, each 7-8 inches wide and 7 feet long. During takeoff, the two front upper rotors are used simultaneously, so it only needs to taxi for 30-40 yards before the fuselage can leave the ground. When landing, the tires touch down, and it can stop within 3-5 yards. It would even be possible to take off and land on a larger rooftop. Although the aircraft's speed is not very high, its ability to hover in the air for some time due to the upward-pointing rotor is particularly valuable. The aircraft weighs only 1,281 pounds, and one person can push it out of the hangar. It can carry 264 pounds of fuel and oil, with a maximum payload of 1,900 pounds. After two demonstration flights, Mr. Peng Te, director of the aviation department of the China Aviation Corporation, was invited for the first test ride.

Features of the Aircraft

The Autogiro aircraft also has the following features: (1) It can be used for transportation and is more suitable for passenger transport. The interior of the aircraft has foldable seats, which can be folded up to carry cargo. (2) Whether transporting cargo, passengers, or mail, it can arrive on time within a certain period. (3) It can be used for security purposes. (4) It can be used for bombing. (5) It can be used for sowing seeds. (6) It can be used for reconnaissance. (7) It does not require a fixed route. (8) It can be used for scientific exploration, etc. The aircraft is equipped with a 140-horsepower engine, with a speed of 90-95 miles per hour, and a maximum speed of 110-115 miles per hour.

Brief History of the Invention

The Autogiro aircraft was invented by Señor don Juan de la Cierva. He began research in 1919, first made the machinery in 1924, and succeeded in 1925. In the same year, the Aivelo Company began manufacturing it. The test flight yesterday was piloted by the famous pilot Lieutenant L.D. Pennett, with more than a dozen reporters from Chinese and foreign newspapers attending.

However, according to the person in charge of the preparatory office, if the public offering is not fully subscribed, the promoters will make up the difference. Xinjiang Steamer Ready After Rectification: Resumes Shanghai-Ningbo Route Today, Regular Stewards Will Be Re-employed, Stewards' Representatives Petitioned Yesterday 116

According to the Ta Kung News Agency, the state-run China Merchants Bureau's Xinjiang Steamer has temporarily suspended sailing to rectify the stewards and eliminate bad habits. All regular stewards have been registered in accordance with the regulations, and the bureau issued badges yesterday, deciding to re-employ all of them. However, they will be paid a monthly salary of 16 yuan, and will not be allowed to solicit tips from passengers in the future. If such behavior occurs, they will be dismissed upon discovery. The bureau also found that the arrangement of bunks in various parts of the ship was not uniform, so it hired workers to dismantle them the night before last, and will re-install them according to the situation, in order to make them tidy and benefit travelers. The ship is scheduled to resume sailing today. A group of stewards formed a petition group. All stewards of the ship said that they were willing to accept this order of rectification by the bureau, as it concerned administration, and there was no resistance. However, they requested improvement because the measures were too strict and would have a great impact on their livelihoods in the future, in order to provide relief. At 7 a.m. yesterday, a joint meeting of cadres and team leaders was held at the Seamen's Anlu Association in Xiaonanmen. Zhao Ruilong was elected chairman. First, the chairman reported that all workers should unanimously support this rectification by the bureau, but the bureau should still consider the workers' difficulties and make improvements where there are major obstacles to their livelihoods. Therefore, a meeting was convened to discuss solutions. The following resolutions were passed: (1) Organize a petition delegation of stewards from the Xinjiang Steamer, and elect Hu Baoquan, Ni Amao, Wang Mingbao, Zhou Longdao, Zhao Ruilong, Li Quangen, Li Baoyuan, Sun Ayuan, and nine others as representatives. (2) All workers should listen to the command of the delegation and should not act without authorization. (3) Issue a declaration to all sectors of society, stating the workers' suffering and requesting understanding. The first meeting of the delegation was held in the afternoon, with all representatives present. Chairman Zhou Longdao resolved: (1) The bureau will issue badges this afternoon, and Committee Member Yang of the Seamen's Association will be asked to collect them and distribute them to the workers. (2) Continue to appeal to all parties, demanding to maintain the original living conditions.

Stating Suffering: The delegation went to the China Merchants Bureau at 3 p.m. yesterday to petition General Manager Liu Hongsheng, stating the workers' suffering, saying, in brief, that all workers accepted the bureau's rectification of discipline, but the fixed wages were meager. According to the previous income from tips, each person earned about 30-40 yuan. Now, suddenly changing to a salary of 16 yuan is equivalent to cutting more than half, which will be difficult for the workers to maintain their livelihoods. Therefore, they requested that ways be found to improve the situation. It is reported that the delegation also plans to appeal to all parties for assistance in maintaining their livelihoods.

It is reported that the total amount of the two types of bond interest is more than 20,000 yuan.

Working on Sunday

The current congress will be held at 1 p.m. on the 23rd, which falls on a Sunday, when offices are usually closed. Now, because the congress is being held, the Standing Committee has notified all sections that they will operate as usual on that day.

Students of the Municipal Party Department's Workers' Training Institute Held Graduation Ceremony Yesterday Morning: Representatives of Party and Government Agencies Attended and Gave Instructions, Deputy Director Zhu Xuefan Issued Certificates 120

According to the Ta Kung News Agency, the first class of students from the Workers' Movement Training Institute, organized by the Municipal Party Department, held a graduation ceremony at Qiaojia Hongmei Family Park at 10 a.m. yesterday. Lu Jingshi and Zhou Lianze from the Municipal Party Department, Cai Jinjun (representing Jin Dianyang) from the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Tu Jiyi from the Security Office, Wang Gang from the Social Affairs Bureau, Pan Gongzhan (representing Jiang Jianbai) from the Education Bureau, Zhou Xuexiang and Ye Xianggao from the General Labor Union, Ye Guanqian from the District Party Department, Xiao Huiqing from the Municipal Farmers' Association, Yu Songqiao and Xu Duo from the Postal Workers' Union, and representatives from various labor unions such as the shipbuilding industry in District 1 and the cotton weaving industry in District 10, totaling more than 200 students, were received by Deputy Director Zhu Xuefan, Training Director Zhao Shusheng, and Education Director Wen Zhuangyou. The postal workers' band provided music.

Chairman's Report

After the ceremony, Zhu Xuefan gave a report on behalf of Director Wu Xingya, saying that he was deeply moved by the representatives of the Party and government agencies and various labor unions attending. The Workers' Movement Training Institute was established by the Municipal Party Department and has been under the leadership of Director Wu for more than five months. With the support of all parties and the guidance of teachers and instructors, we are holding a graduation ceremony here today. In the past history of the Chinese workers' movement, there has always been a lack of talent and a lack of organization. There has been no sufficient representation of power for society and the country. However, the workers' movement occupies an important position in the modern revolutionary process, not only limited to assisting the use of military and political power, but also greatly related to economic resources and the prosperity and decline of industry and commerce. Looking back on the past closures of yarn and silk factories, social economics have formed an unease, the state of affairs is chaotic, and the spirit of the people is depressed. The purpose and expectation of the training institute organized by the Municipal Party Department is to create a group of passionate young people to fight for the country, sacrifice for society, save the country from danger, and promote the workers' movement. After all the students graduate and leave school, they will step into the social journey, seek a living, and at the same time, start leading the workers' movement. He hoped that the superiors would provide guidance from time to time to correct deficiencies. On the one hand, he hoped that all students would apply their school experience and knowledge to society, and be determined to be hardworking and resilient, unify their thoughts, be full of spirit, and shoulder the responsibility of saving the country and the nation. In the near future, the Shanghai workers' movement will, after being infused with this new element, be promoted and developed in the face of internal and external troubles, maintaining its permanent atmosphere.

Party Department's Instructions

Lu Jingshi, representing the Municipal Party Department, delivered an instruction speech, saying that since the Workers' Movement Training Institute was established, with the efforts of the director, deputy director, and all the faculty and staff, the training period of five months has been completed. The opening and graduation ceremonies are the same, but their natures are different. Today, on behalf of the Municipal Party Department, I am attending the ceremony to tell the students what I have learned. In this recession, it is most difficult to carry out the workers' movement. In the stage of economic warfare of imperialism in our country, on the one hand, the lives of workers cannot be improved, but even reduced wages, reduced salaries, and increased unemployment, and on the other hand, the output of capital is accumulated, business is sluggish, cleared and closed. The national workers' movement is difficult to develop due to these reasons. All the students have a deep understanding of the social situation. After these months of training, their will is unified and their knowledge is sufficient to deal with it, and they can still achieve excellent results. He hoped that all the students would engage in leading the workers' movement, (1) not seek fame and fortune, but be practical and realistic, (2) not improve their lives, but be thrifty and honest, cultivate morality and personality, (3) have a strong will, not be passive, not be timid, and be full of the spirit of sacrifice and struggle. Then Jiang Jianbai, representing the Municipal Education Bureau, Wang Jiyi, representing the Security Bureau, Zhou Xuexiang from the General Labor Union, and Zhou Lianze gave speeches (the words are omitted).

Students' Reply

After the representatives of the various organizations finished speaking, Deputy Director Zhu Xuefan issued graduation certificates, and then Lu Baozhi, a representative of the students, delivered a reply speech, saying that the instructions and encouragement given by the representatives of the various organizations and the leaders of the labor world were to be taken as golden rules. After graduating and leaving school, they will gradually practice the teachings of the teachers on weekdays, according to various situations. He deeply hoped that the representatives would give instructions and guidance at any time, and he was very grateful.

Ministry of Communications Announces: Revised Organizational Charter of the China Merchants Bureau 121

The Ministry of Communications recently amended Articles 17, 35, 37, 38, 39, 40, 47, 61, 63, 64, 65, and 66 of the organizational charter of the state-run China Merchants Bureau. Yesterday, it was announced by ministerial order as follows: (Article 17) The Supervisory Board shall have one secretary and two to three auditors, and two clerks, who shall be selected by the chairman and submitted to the Supervisory Board for resolution and appointment, and reported to the Ministry of Communications for record. (Article 35) The General Manager's Office shall manage the General Affairs, Business, and Shipping Sections, and the Treasury. (Article 37) The Business Section shall manage the following matters: (1) Matters concerning the allocation, dispatch, and planning of ships on various routes; (2) Matters concerning the investigation of shipping market conditions; (3) Matters concerning the scheduling of ships and the notification of loading and unloading of goods; (4) Matters concerning the solicitation and handling of passengers and goods; (5) Matters that should be handled to facilitate passengers; (6) Matters concerning the joint transport of passengers and goods; (7) Matters concerning the establishment of freight rates; (8) Matters concerning the establishment of passenger ticket rates; (9) Matters concerning the establishment of passenger commission rates; (10) Matters concerning liaising with the customs; (11) Matters concerning the issuance of advertisements; (12) Matters concerning the assessment of the business of various ships; (13) Matters concerning the assessment of the business of branch offices; (14) Matters concerning liaison with the same industry; (15) Matters concerning the management of inland river shipping; (16) Matters concerning the rental of ships; (17) Matters concerning compensation for transportation damages; (18) Matters concerning the solicitation of business for wharves and warehouses and the storage of goods; (19) Matters concerning the clearing of goods in the warehouse; (20) Matters concerning the establishment of rental rates for wharves and warehouses; (21) Matters concerning the establishment of loading rates; (22) Matters concerning the management, assessment, promotion, and demotion of wharf and warehouse personnel; (23) Matters concerning the management of wharf inspectors and patrols; (24) Matters concerning the construction supervision and acceptance of wharves, warehouses, and ships; (25) Matters concerning the cleanliness, fire protection, and other equipment of wharves; (26) Matters concerning the management of coal yards. (Article 38) The Shipping Section shall manage the following matters: (1) Matters concerning the jurisdiction of ship driving and mechanical personnel, and the allocation of their duties; (2) Matters concerning the management, promotion, demotion, and registration of sailors; (3) Matters concerning the inspection of ship hulls and machinery; (4) Matters concerning the repair supervision and acceptance of ships; (5) Matters concerning the equipment and hygiene of ships; (6) Matters concerning the bidding and acceptance of various ship projects; (7) Matters concerning the management of the China Merchants Machinery Factory, and the assessment of its personnel; (8) Matters concerning the establishment and management of ship radio, and the assessment of its personnel; (9) Matters concerning the acceptance of coal materials used by ships; (10) Matters concerning the fire protection and rescue of ships; (11) Other ship matters. (Article 39) The Treasury shall manage the following matters: (1) Matters concerning the receipt and disbursement of cash; (2) Matters concerning the registration of cash receipt and disbursement books and bank transaction books; (3) Matters concerning the custody of cash and bank transaction vouchers and checks; (4) Matters concerning the custody of the Bureau's real estate documents, loan contracts, and business contracts. (Article 40) The General Manager's Office, each section, and the Treasury shall each have one director who shall accept the orders of the General Manager and preside over the affairs of the section. More complex sections may have one to two deputy directors to assist the director. (Article 47) The secretaries of the General Manager's Office, the directors and deputy directors of each section, the director of the Treasury, and the inspectors shall be proposed by the General Manager, resolved by the Board of Directors, and submitted to the Ministry of Communications for approval before appointment. (Article 62) The accounting affairs of the Bureau shall be managed by the Accounting Office. The rules shall be formulated separately. (Article 63) The rules of procedure for the Supervisory Board and the Board of Directors shall be formulated by the respective boards and submitted to the Ministry of Communications for approval. (Article 64) The rules of procedure for the General Manager's Office, branch offices, and offices shall be formulated by the General Manager's Office, submitted to the Board of Directors for resolution, and submitted to the Ministry of Communications for approval. The purchasing regulations, accounting regulations, employee bond regulations, and compensation regulations shall be the same. (Article 65) The distribution of the Bureau's annual surplus shall be proposed by the General Manager, resolved by the Board of Directors, and submitted to the Ministry of Communications for approval. (Article 66) This Charter shall take effect from the date of promulgation.

Municipal Health Bureau: Inspects Summer Drinks, Many Are Harmful to Health, Citizens Should Pay Attention 125

In order to prevent gastrointestinal infectious diseases such as cholera, typhoid fever, and dysentery, the Health Bureau pays close attention to the soft drinks and other refreshing drinks sold on the market in the summer. Because there are many varieties and many people drink them, if they are not pure, they will greatly harm the health of drinkers. However, whether these beverages are pure or not can only be accurately judged after inspection. Therefore, the Health Bureau ordered the Health Testing Institute to collect as many soft drinks and vegetable seed dew as possible sold on the market and inspect them in detail. It has now inspected 21 types of soft drinks, and only Coca-Cola, Russian, Meiguli, and Kuzhe soft drinks have passed the inspection. It has inspected 44 types of vegetable seed dew, and only the Black Gauze House vegetable seed dew and the China Food Company's Star and Moon brand banana fruit dew have passed the inspection. A total of 3 types of sour plum juice have been inspected, but only one has passed. All those that did not pass had too many bacteria and did not meet the standards for municipal refreshing drinks. If they contain germs, it is easier to get sick after drinking them. The Health Bureau has notified the manufacturers of those that did not pass the inspection to make practical improvements so that they can be inspected again. If germs are found after inspection, they will be banned from sale.
